<link rel="canonical" href="https://patents.google.com/patent/CN221936334U/en">
<meta name="description" content="
The present application discloses an electric tool. The electric tool includes an output shaft, a brushless motor, a transmission mechanism, a gripping part, a control component and an anti-electromagnetic interference device. The output shaft is used to drive the working accessory to move. The brushless motor is provided with or connected to a motor shaft. The transmission mechanism is used to realize transmission between the motor shaft and the output shaft. The gripping part is for the user to hold. The control component includes a circuit board component and circuit elements. The anti-electromagnetic interference device includes an anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board for suppressing electromagnetic interference. The minimum distance between the circuit board component and the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board is greater than or equal to 5mm. The electric tool is anti-electromagnetic interference device and the control component are separately arranged, so that the electromagnetic interference device and the control component can make full use of the space inside the electric tool for layout, which is conducive to the miniaturization of the electric tool.
">

<section itemprop="abstract" itemscope>
<h2>Abstract</h2>
<aside>Translated from <span itemprop="translatedLanguage">Chinese</span></aside>
<div itemprop="content" html><abstract mxw-id="PA696374846" lang="EN" load-source="google">
<span class="notranslate">
<span class="google-src-text">
<p num="0001">本申请公开了一种电动工具。该电动工具包括输出轴、无刷电机、传动机构、握持部、控制组件和抗电磁干扰器件，输出轴用于驱动工作附件运动，无刷电机设有或连接有一个电机轴，传动机构用于在电机轴与输出轴之间实现传动，握持部供用户握持，控制组件包括电路板组件和电路元件，抗电磁干扰器件，包括抗电磁干扰电路板，用于抑制电磁干扰，电路板组件与抗电磁干扰电路板之间的最小距离大于或等于5mm。该电动工具抗通过将电磁干扰器件与控制组件分别单独设置，使得电磁干扰器件与控制组件能够充分利用电动工具内部的空间进行布局，利于实现电动工具的小型化。</p>
<span class="patent-image-not-available"></span>
</span>
<p num="0001">The present application discloses an electric tool. The electric tool includes an output shaft, a brushless motor, a transmission mechanism, a gripping part, a control component and an anti-electromagnetic interference device. The output shaft is used to drive the working accessory to move. The brushless motor is provided with or connected to a motor shaft. The transmission mechanism is used to realize transmission between the motor shaft and the output shaft. The gripping part is for the user to hold. The control component includes a circuit board component and circuit elements. The anti-electromagnetic interference device includes an anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board for suppressing electromagnetic interference. The minimum distance between the circuit board component and the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board is greater than or equal to 5mm. The electric tool is anti-electromagnetic interference device and the control component are separately arranged, so that the electromagnetic interference device and the control component can make full use of the space inside the electric tool for layout, which is conducive to the miniaturization of the electric tool.</p>
<span class="patent-image-not-available"></span>
</span>
</abstract>
</div>
</section>

<section itemprop="description" itemscope>
<h2>Description</h2>
<aside>Translated from <span itemprop="translatedLanguage">Chinese</span></aside>
<div itemprop="content" html><description mxw-id="PDES478881954" lang="EN" load-source="google">
<invention-title lang="ZH" id="title1">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">电动工具</span>Power Tools</span>
</invention-title>
<technical-field>
<p id="p0001">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">技术领域</span>Technical Field</span>
</p>
<p id="p0002" num="0001">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">本申请涉及一种电动工具，具体涉及一种电动工具。</span>The present application relates to an electric tool, and in particular to an electric tool.</span>
</p>
</technical-field>
<background-art>
<p id="p0003">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">背景技术</span>Background Art</span>
</p>
<p id="p0004" num="0002">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">相关技术中的抛光机是一种利用电动机驱动抛光盘高速旋转，使得抛光盘对工件的待抛光表面进行抛光作业的打磨工具。抛光机也称为研磨机，常用于机械式打磨、抛光以及打蜡，抛光盘包括海绵以及羊毛抛光盘，在抛光盘和抛光剂的共同作用下对待抛光表面进行摩擦，从而能够达到去除漆面污染、氧化层、浅痕的目的。</span>A polishing machine in the related art is a grinding tool that uses a motor to drive a polishing disc to rotate at high speed, so that the polishing disc polishes the surface of the workpiece to be polished. A polishing machine is also called a grinder, which is commonly used for mechanical grinding, polishing and waxing. The polishing disc includes a sponge and a wool polishing disc. The polishing disc and the polishing agent rub the surface to be polished, thereby removing paint pollution, oxide layer, and shallow marks.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0005" num="0003">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">抛光机具有用于实现控制的控制组件，现有抛光机的控制组件包括两个或者两个以上的PCB板，从而导致控制组件的占用空间较大，不利于实现抛光机的小型化。</span>The polishing machine has a control component for realizing control. The control component of the existing polishing machine includes two or more PCB boards, which results in that the control component occupies a large space, which is not conducive to realizing the miniaturization of the polishing machine.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0006" num="0004">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">本部分提供了与本申请相关的背景信息，这些背景信息不一定是现有技术。</span>This section provides background information related to the present application which is not necessarily prior art.</span>
</p>
</background-art>
<disclosure>
<p id="p0007">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">实用新型内容</span>Utility Model Content</span>
</p>
<p id="p0008" num="0005">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">本申请的一个目的是解决或至少减轻上述问题的一部分或者全部。为此，本申请的一个目的在于提供一种电动工具，该电动工具的布局合理，使得电动工具小型化。</span>One object of the present application is to solve or at least alleviate part or all of the above problems. To this end, one object of the present application is to provide an electric tool with a reasonable layout, so that the electric tool is miniaturized.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0009" num="0006">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">为了实现上述目标，本申请采用如下的技术方案：</span>In order to achieve the above objectives, this application adopts the following technical solutions:</span>
</p>
<p id="p0010" num="0007">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">一种电动工具，包括：输出轴，用于驱动工作附件运动；无刷电机，设有或连接有一个电机轴；传动机构，用于在所述电机轴与所述输出轴之间实现传动；握持部，供用户握持；控制组件，包括电路板组件和电路元件；抗电磁干扰器件，包括抗电磁干扰电路板，用于抑制电磁干扰；所述抗电磁干扰器件与所述控制组件分别单独设置，所述电路板组件与所述抗电磁干扰电路板之间的最小距离大于或等于5mm。</span>An electric tool comprises: an output shaft for driving a working accessory to move; a brushless motor provided with or connected to a motor shaft; a transmission mechanism for realizing transmission between the motor shaft and the output shaft; a grip for a user to hold; a control assembly comprising a circuit board assembly and circuit elements; an anti-electromagnetic interference device comprising an anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board for suppressing electromagnetic interference; the anti-electromagnetic interference device and the control assembly are separately arranged, and the minimum distance between the circuit board assembly and the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board is greater than or equal to 5 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0011" num="0008">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，所述抗电磁干扰器件与所述控制组件之间的最小距离大于或等于10mm。</span>In some embodiments, the minimum distance between the anti-electromagnetic interference device and the control component is greater than or equal to 10 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0012" num="0009">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，所述电动工具还包括供用户操作以控制所述无刷电机启停的电机开关，所述电机开关设置在所述抗电磁干扰器件与所述控制组件之间。</span>In some embodiments, the electric tool further includes a motor switch for a user to operate to control the start and stop of the brushless motor, and the motor switch is disposed between the anti-electromagnetic interference device and the control component.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0013" num="0010">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，所述电动工具还包括调速器，所述调速器用于调节所述无刷电机的转速。</span>In some embodiments, the electric tool further includes a speed regulator, which is used to adjust the rotation speed of the brushless motor.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0014" num="0011">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，沿所述握持部延伸方向上，所述调速器和所述控制组件至少部分重叠。</span>In some embodiments, along the extension direction of the grip portion, the speed regulator and the control assembly at least partially overlap.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0015" num="0012">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，所述电动工具还包括供用户操作以控制所述无刷电机启停的电机开关，所述调速器位于所述电机开关和所述无刷电机之间。</span>In some embodiments, the electric tool further comprises a motor switch for a user to operate to control the start and stop of the brushless motor, and the speed regulator is located between the motor switch and the brushless motor.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0016" num="0013">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，所述抗电磁干扰器件包括第一电容、电阻和电感，所述第一电容、所述电阻和所述电感均集成在所述抗电磁干扰电路板上。</span>In some embodiments, the anti-electromagnetic interference device includes a first capacitor, a resistor, and an inductor, and the first capacitor, the resistor, and the inductor are all integrated on the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0017" num="0014">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，所述抗电磁干扰电路板的最大长度小于65mm。</span>In some embodiments, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board is less than 65 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0018" num="0015">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，所述抗电磁干扰电路板的最大长度小于55mm。</span>In some embodiments, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board is less than 55 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0019" num="0016">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，所述抗电磁干扰电路板的最大长度小于45mm。</span>In some embodiments, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board is less than 45 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0020" num="0017">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">本申请的有益之处在于：</span>The benefits of this application are:</span>
</p>
<p id="p0021" num="0018">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">本申请提供的电动工具包括输出轴、无刷电机、传动机构、握持部、控制组件和抗电磁干扰器件，输出轴用于驱动工作附件运动，无刷电机设有或连接有一个电机轴，传动机构用于在电机轴与输出轴之间实现传动，握持部供用户握持，控制组件包括电路板组件和电路元件，抗电磁干扰器件包括抗电磁干扰电路板，用于抑制电磁干扰，电路板组件与抗电磁干扰电路板之间的最小距离大于或等于5mm。该电动工具抗通过将电磁干扰器件与控制组件分别单独设置，使得电磁干扰器件与控制组件能够充分利用电动工具内部的空间进行布局，利于实现电动工具的小型化。</span>The electric tool provided by the present application includes an output shaft, a brushless motor, a transmission mechanism, a gripping part, a control component and an anti-electromagnetic interference device, wherein the output shaft is used to drive the working accessory to move, the brushless motor is provided with or connected to a motor shaft, the transmission mechanism is used to realize transmission between the motor shaft and the output shaft, the gripping part is for the user to hold, the control component includes a circuit board component and circuit elements, the anti-electromagnetic interference device includes an anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board for suppressing electromagnetic interference, and the minimum distance between the circuit board component and the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board is greater than or equal to 5mm. The electric tool is anti-electromagnetic interference device and the control component are separately arranged, so that the electromagnetic interference device and the control component can make full use of the space inside the electric tool for layout, which is conducive to the miniaturization of the electric tool.</span>
</p>
</disclosure>

<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">具体实施方式</span>DETAILED DESCRIPTION</span>
</p>
<p id="p0063" num="0058">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在详细解释本申请的任何实施方式之前，应当理解，本申请不限于其应用到以下描述中阐述的或以上附图中所示的结构细节和组件布置。</span>Before any embodiments of the application are explained in detail, it is to be understood that the application is not limited in its application to the details of construction and the arrangement of components set forth in the following description or illustrated in the above drawings.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0064" num="0059">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在本申请中，术语“包括”、“包含”、“具有”或者其任何其他变体意在涵盖非排他性的包含，从而使得包括一系列要素的过程、方法、物品或者装置不仅包括那些要素，而且还包括没有明确列出的其他要素，或者是还包括为这种过程、方法、物品或者装置所固有的要素。在没有更多限制的情况下，由语句“包括一个……”限定的要素，并不排除在包括该要素的过程、方法、物品或者装置中还存在另外的相同要素。</span>In this application, the terms &#34;comprises&#34;, &#34;includes&#34;, &#34;has&#34; or any other variations thereof are intended to cover non-exclusive inclusion, so that a process, method, article or device that includes a series of elements includes not only those elements, but also includes other elements not explicitly listed, or also includes elements inherent to such process, method, article or device. In the absence of more restrictions, an element defined by the sentence &#34;comprises a ...&#34; does not exclude the presence of other identical elements in the process, method, article or device that includes the element.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0065" num="0060">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在本申请中，术语“和/或”，是一种描述关联对象的关联关系，表示可以存在三种关系。例如，A和/或B，可以表示：单独存在A，同时存在A和B，单独存在B这三种情况。另外，本申请中字符“/”，一般表示前后关联对象是一种“和/或”的关系。</span>In this application, the term &#34;and/or&#34; is a description of the association relationship between related objects, indicating that three relationships can exist. For example, A and/or B can represent: A exists alone, A and B exist at the same time, and B exists alone. In addition, the character &#34;/&#34; in this application generally indicates that the related objects before and after are in an &#34;and/or&#34; relationship.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0066" num="0061">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">本申请中，术语“连接”、“结合”、“耦合”、“安装”可以是直接连接、结合、耦合或安装，也可以是间接连接、结合、耦合或安装。其中，进行举例示范，直接连接指的是两个零件或组件之间不需设置中间件而连接在一起，间接连接指的是两个零件或组件分别与至少一个中间件连接，这两个零件或组件通过中间件实现连接。此外，“连接”和“耦合”不限于物理或机械连接或耦合，并且可以包括电连接或耦合。</span>In the present application, the terms &#34;connect&#34;, &#34;combine&#34;, &#34;couple&#34;, and &#34;install&#34; may refer to direct connection, combination, coupling, or installation, or indirect connection, combination, coupling, or installation. For example, direct connection refers to two parts or components being connected together without the need for an intermediate piece, and indirect connection refers to two parts or components being connected to at least one intermediate piece respectively, and the two parts or components being connected via the intermediate piece. In addition, &#34;connect&#34; and &#34;couple&#34; are not limited to physical or mechanical connections or couplings, and may include electrical connections or couplings.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0067" num="0062">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在本申请中，本领域普通技术人员将理解，结合数量或条件使用的相对术语(例如，“约”，“大约”，“基本”等)为包括所述值并且具有上下文所指示的含义。例如，该相对术语至少包括与特定值的测量相关的误差程度，与特定值相关的由制造，组装，使用造成的公差等。这种术语也应被视为公开了由两个端点的绝对值限定的范围。相对术语可指代所指示的值的一定百分比(例如1％，5％，10％或更多)的加或减。未采用相对术语的数值，也应该被揭示为具有公差的特定值。此外，“基本”在表达相对的角度位置关系时(例如，基本平行，基本垂直)，可指代在所指示的角度的基础上加或减一定度数(例如1度，5度，10度或更多)。</span>In the present application, it will be understood by those of ordinary skill in the art that relative terms (e.g., &#34;about,&#34; &#34;approximately,&#34; &#34;substantially,&#34; etc.) used in conjunction with quantities or conditions include the values and have the meaning indicated by the context. For example, the relative terms include at least the degree of error associated with the measurement of a specific value, the tolerances caused by manufacturing, assembly, and use associated with a specific value, and the like. Such terms should also be considered to disclose a range defined by the absolute values of the two endpoints. Relative terms may refer to plus or minus a certain percentage (e.g., 1%, 5%, 10% or more) of the indicated value. Numerical values that do not use relative terms should also be disclosed as specific values with tolerances. In addition, &#34;substantially&#34; may refer to plus or minus a certain degree (e.g., 1 degree, 5 degrees, 10 degrees or more) on the basis of the indicated angle when expressing a relative angular position relationship (e.g., substantially parallel, substantially perpendicular).</span>
</p>
<p id="p0068" num="0063">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在本申请中，本领域普通技术人员将理解，由组件执行的功能可以为由一个组件，多个组件，一个零件，或多个零件执行。同样的，由零件执行的功能也可以由一个零件，一个组件，或多个零件组合来执行。</span>In this application, it will be understood by those skilled in the art that the function performed by a component can be performed by one component, multiple components, one part, or multiple parts. Similarly, the function performed by a part can also be performed by one part, one component, or a combination of multiple parts.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0069" num="0064">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在本申请中，术语“上”、“下”、“左”、“右”、“前”、“后”等方位词是以附图所示的方位和位置关系来进行描述的，不应理解为对本申请实施例的限定。此外，在上下文中，还需要理解的是，当提到一个元件连接在另一个元件“上”或者“下”时，其不仅能够直接连接在另一个元件“上”或者“下”，也可以通过中间元件间接连接在另一个元件“上”或者“下”。还应当理解的，上侧、下侧、左侧、右侧、前侧、后侧等方位词不仅代表正方位，也可以理解为侧方位。例如，下方可以包括正下方、左下方、右下方、前下方以及后下方等。</span>In the present application, the terms &#34;upper&#34;, &#34;lower&#34;, &#34;left&#34;, &#34;right&#34;, &#34;front&#34;, &#34;back&#34; and other directional words are described based on the orientation and positional relationship shown in the accompanying drawings, and should not be understood as limiting the embodiments of the present application. In addition, in the context, it is also necessary to understand that when it is mentioned that an element is connected to another element &#34;upper&#34; or &#34;lower&#34;, it can not only be directly connected to another element &#34;upper&#34; or &#34;lower&#34;, but also indirectly connected to another element &#34;upper&#34; or &#34;lower&#34; through an intermediate element. It should also be understood that directional words such as upper side, lower side, left side, right side, front side, back side, etc. not only represent the positive orientation, but can also be understood as the lateral orientation. For example, the bottom can include directly below, lower left, lower right, lower front, and lower back, etc.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0070" num="0065">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在本申请中，术语“控制器”、“处理器”、“中央处理器”、“CPU”、“MCU”可以互换。在使用单元“控制器”、“处理器”、“中央处理器”、“CPU”、或“MCU”来执行特定功能，除非另有说明，否则这些功能则可以由单个上述单元或多个上述单元来执行。</span>In this application, the terms &#34;controller&#34;, &#34;processor&#34;, &#34;central processing unit&#34;, &#34;CPU&#34;, and &#34;MCU&#34; are interchangeable. When a unit &#34;controller&#34;, &#34;processor&#34;, &#34;central processing unit&#34;, &#34;CPU&#34;, or &#34;MCU&#34; is used to perform a specific function, unless otherwise specified, these functions can be performed by a single unit or multiple units.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0071" num="0066">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在本申请中，术语“装置”、“模块”或“单元”为了实现特定的功能，它们可以通过硬件或软件的形式来实现。</span>In the present application, the terms &#34;device&#34;, &#34;module&#34; or &#34;unit&#34; may be implemented in the form of hardware or software to achieve specific functions.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0072" num="0067">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在本申请中，术语“计算”、“判断”、“控制”、“确定”、“识别”等指的是计算机系统或类似电子计算设备(例如，控制器，处理器等)的操作和过程。</span>In this application, the terms &#34;calculate&#34;, &#34;judge&#34;, &#34;control&#34;, &#34;determine&#34;, &#34;identify&#34;, etc. refer to the operations and processes of a computer system or similar electronic computing device (e.g., controller, processor, etc.).</span>
</p>
<p id="p0073" num="0068">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">本申请提供了一种电动工具，在一些实施例中，电动工具可以为交流抛光机，当然在其他实施例中，根据需要可以通过更换作业附件，使得该电动工具成为可以为执行其他作业的工具，例如，冲击钻、电动螺丝批等。</span>The present application provides an electric tool. In some embodiments, the electric tool may be an AC polisher. Of course, in other embodiments, the electric tool may be replaced with operating accessories as needed to enable the electric tool to be a tool for performing other operations, such as an impact drill, an electric screwdriver, etc.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0074" num="0069">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">如图1至图6所示，该电动工具包括机壳10、无刷电机14、传动机构15、输出轴12、工作附件13、风扇16、控制组件20、抗电磁干扰器件30和调速器40。</span>As shown in FIGS. 1 to 6 , the electric tool includes a housing 10 , a brushless motor 14 , a transmission mechanism 15 , an output shaft 12 , a working accessory 13 , a fan 16 , a control component 20 , an anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and a speed regulator 40 .</span>
</p>
<p id="p0075" num="0070">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">机壳10是电动工具主要的安装部件和防护部件，机壳10可以为一体成型件，也可以由多个部分连接形成。如图2所示，机壳10包括第一壳体101、第二壳体102和第三壳体103。其中，第一壳体101和第二壳体102均为半壳，第一壳体101和第二壳体102左右拼接形成机壳10的后壳体，控制组件20、抗电磁干扰器件30和调速器40均安装在后壳体内，后壳体的后部形成供电源线17伸入的通孔。第三壳体103为电动工具的前壳体，第三壳体103可以为由两个半壳拼接形成，也可以为一体成型件，传动机构15以及输出轴12的顶部置于第三壳体103内，第三壳体103的下部形成供输出轴12伸出的通孔。</span>The housing 10 is the main installation component and protective component of the power tool. The housing 10 can be an integral part or can be formed by connecting multiple parts. As shown in Figure 2, the housing 10 includes a first shell 101, a second shell 102 and a third shell 103. Among them, the first shell 101 and the second shell 102 are both half shells. The first shell 101 and the second shell 102 are spliced left and right to form the rear shell of the housing 10. The control component 20, the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the speed regulator 40 are all installed in the rear shell. The rear part of the rear shell forms a through hole for the power cord 17 to extend into. The third shell 103 is the front shell of the power tool. The third shell 103 can be formed by splicing two half shells or an integral part. The transmission mechanism 15 and the top of the output shaft 12 are placed in the third shell 103, and the lower part of the third shell 103 forms a through hole for the output shaft 12 to extend out.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0076" num="0071">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">机壳10部分形成供用户握持的握持部11，用户握持握持部11以操作该电动工具。在一些实施例中，后壳体部分即为握持部11，在握持部11上设置有防滑结构，以提高用户握持握持部11的稳定性，防滑结构可以为防滑胶套、防滑纹路等。</span>The housing 10 is partially formed into a grip 11 for the user to hold, and the user holds the grip 11 to operate the power tool. In some embodiments, the rear housing portion is the grip 11, and an anti-slip structure is provided on the grip 11 to improve the stability of the user holding the grip 11. The anti-slip structure can be an anti-slip rubber sleeve, anti-slip texture, etc.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0077" num="0072">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，如图3所示，握持部11沿中分线处的周长D1小于135mm。在一个实施例中，握持部11沿中分线处的周长D1为133mm；在一个实施例中，握持部11沿中分线处的周长D1为130mm；在一个实施例中，握持部11沿中分线处的周长D1为127mm；在一个实施例中，握持部11沿中分线处的周长D1为122mm；在一个实施例中，握持部11沿中分线处的周长D1为119mm；在一个实施例中，握持部11沿中分线处的周长D1为115mm。</span>In some embodiments, as shown in FIG3 , the perimeter D1 of the grip portion 11 along the midline is less than 135 mm. In one embodiment, the perimeter D1 of the grip portion 11 along the midline is 133 mm; in one embodiment, the perimeter D1 of the grip portion 11 along the midline is 130 mm; in one embodiment, the perimeter D1 of the grip portion 11 along the midline is 127 mm; in one embodiment, the perimeter D1 of the grip portion 11 along the midline is 122 mm; in one embodiment, the perimeter D1 of the grip portion 11 along the midline is 119 mm; in one embodiment, the perimeter D1 of the grip portion 11 along the midline is 115 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0078" num="0073">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">无刷电机14置于机壳10内，具体地，无刷电机14可以置于前壳体内，也可以置于后壳体内。在一些并列的实施例中，无刷电机14的电机外壳144外置成为机壳10的一部分，电机外壳144连接于前壳体和后壳体之间。</span>The brushless motor 14 is placed in the housing 10. Specifically, the brushless motor 14 can be placed in the front housing or in the rear housing. In some parallel embodiments, the motor housing 144 of the brushless motor 14 is externally placed as a part of the housing 10, and the motor housing 144 is connected between the front housing and the rear housing.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0079" num="0074">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">无刷电机14除了包括电机外壳144外，还包括设置在电机外壳144内的定子142、转子143、轴承组件等。在一些实施例中，无刷电机14的轴承组件包括支撑在电机轴141前端的第一轴承145，第一轴承145与无刷电机14的定子142在电机轴141的轴线方向上至少部分重叠。如此设置可提高电动工具内部的紧凑性，有利于实现电动工具的小型化。</span>In addition to the motor housing 144, the brushless motor 14 also includes a stator 142, a rotor 143, a bearing assembly, etc. disposed in the motor housing 144. In some embodiments, the bearing assembly of the brushless motor 14 includes a first bearing 145 supported at the front end of the motor shaft 141, and the first bearing 145 and the stator 142 of the brushless motor 14 at least partially overlap in the axial direction of the motor shaft 141. Such a configuration can improve the compactness of the interior of the power tool, which is conducive to miniaturization of the power tool.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0080" num="0075">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个具体的实施例中，本申请通过将固定第一轴承145的轴承定位结构向电机外壳144内侧移动15mm至定子142里面；在其他实施例中，该移动的距离根据需求还可以进行调整。轴承定位结构可以为轴承座或者定位槽。</span>In a specific embodiment, the present application moves the bearing positioning structure that fixes the first bearing 145 15 mm to the inside of the motor housing 144 to the inside of the stator 142; in other embodiments, the moving distance can be adjusted according to needs. The bearing positioning structure can be a bearing seat or a positioning groove.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0081" num="0076">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图5和图6所示，风扇16套设在电机轴141上，且风扇16位于无刷电机14和控制组件20之间。在一些实施例中，风扇16套设在无刷电机14的电机轴141的后端，无刷电机14的轴承组件还包括支撑在电机轴141后端的第二轴承146，第二轴承146与风扇16在电机轴141的轴线方向上至少部分重叠。</span>5 and 6 , the fan 16 is sleeved on the motor shaft 141, and the fan 16 is located between the brushless motor 14 and the control assembly 20. In some embodiments, the fan 16 is sleeved on the rear end of the motor shaft 141 of the brushless motor 14, and the bearing assembly of the brushless motor 14 further includes a second bearing 146 supported on the rear end of the motor shaft 141, and the second bearing 146 at least partially overlaps with the fan 16 in the axial direction of the motor shaft 141.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0082" num="0077">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个具体的实施例中，本申请通过将固定第二轴承146的轴承定位件147向电机外壳144内侧移动14.5mm至风扇16上内凹腔里面；在其他实施例中，该移动的距离根据需求还可以进行调整。轴承定位件147可以为轴承座或者定位槽。</span>In a specific embodiment, the present application moves the bearing locating member 147 fixing the second bearing 146 14.5 mm to the inner side of the motor housing 144 to the inner concave cavity of the fan 16; in other embodiments, the moving distance can be adjusted according to needs. The bearing locating member 147 can be a bearing seat or a locating groove.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0083" num="0078">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">如图7所示，在一些实施例中，在定子142外还套设有降噪金属环148，降噪金属环148紧贴定子142的外壁面，在减轻定子142震动的同时，实现降噪效果。在一个实施例中，降噪金属环148设置有多个，多个降噪金属环148在无刷电机14的电机轴141方向上间隔设置。</span>As shown in FIG7 , in some embodiments, a noise reduction metal ring 148 is further sleeved outside the stator 142, and the noise reduction metal ring 148 is closely attached to the outer wall surface of the stator 142, thereby reducing the vibration of the stator 142 and achieving a noise reduction effect. In one embodiment, a plurality of noise reduction metal rings 148 are provided, and the plurality of noise reduction metal rings 148 are spaced apart in the direction of the motor shaft 141 of the brushless motor 14.</span>

<p id="p0088" num="0083">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，无刷电机14整机的标称功率大于500W且小于2500W。需要说明的是，标称功率为电动工具的整机功率，具体可以为交流抛光机的整机功率。对于交流抛光机而言，标称功率是指机器铭牌上标示的功率值，也是机器的额定功率值。在一个实施例中，无刷电机14整机的标称功率为800W；在一个实施例中，无刷电机14整机的标称功率为1100W；在一个实施例中，无刷电机14整机的标称功率为1300W；在一个实施例中，无刷电机14整机的标称功率为1600W；在一个实施例中，无刷电机14整机的标称功率为1800W。</span>In some embodiments, the nominal power of the entire brushless motor 14 is greater than 500W and less than 2500W. It should be noted that the nominal power is the entire power of the power tool, specifically the entire power of the AC polishing machine. For an AC polishing machine, the nominal power refers to the power value indicated on the machine nameplate, which is also the rated power value of the machine. In one embodiment, the nominal power of the entire brushless motor 14 is 800W; in one embodiment, the nominal power of the entire brushless motor 14 is 1100W; in one embodiment, the nominal power of the entire brushless motor 14 is 1300W; in one embodiment, the nominal power of the entire brushless motor 14 is 1600W; in one embodiment, the nominal power of the entire brushless motor 14 is 1800W.</span>

<p id="p0090" num="0085">

</p>
<p id="p0091" num="0086">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图4至图6所示，无刷电机14设有或连接有一个电机轴141，传动机构15连接于电机轴141和输出轴12之间，并用于在电机轴141与输出轴12之间实现传动。相较于现有的抛光机使用串激有刷电机的刷碳更换麻烦，本申请通过使用无刷电机14能够有效的解决该问题。</span>4 to 6, the brushless motor 14 is provided with or connected to a motor shaft 141, and the transmission mechanism 15 is connected between the motor shaft 141 and the output shaft 12, and is used to achieve transmission between the motor shaft 141 and the output shaft 12. Compared with the existing polishing machine using a series-excited brush motor, which is troublesome to replace the brush carbon, the present application can effectively solve this problem by using a brushless motor 14.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0092" num="0087">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在电动工具的工作状态下，电机轴141基本水平设置，而输出轴12基本竖直设置，为了实现动力在电机轴141和输出轴12之间的传递，如图6所示，传动机构15包括行星轮组件151、第一锥齿轮152、第二锥齿轮153、第一减速轴154和第二减速轴155，无刷电机14的电机轴141与第一减速轴154同轴连接，第一减速轴154与行星轮组件151的太阳轮连接，第二减速轴155与行星轮组件151的行星架连接，第一锥齿轮152形成或者连接在第二减速轴155上，第二锥齿轮153形成或者连接在输出轴12上。</span>When the power tool is in the working state, the motor shaft 141 is basically arranged horizontally, and the output shaft 12 is basically arranged vertically. In order to realize the transmission of power between the motor shaft 141 and the output shaft 12, as shown in Figure 6, the transmission mechanism 15 includes a planetary gear assembly 151, a first bevel gear 152, a second bevel gear 153, a first reduction shaft 154 and a second reduction shaft 155. The motor shaft 141 of the brushless motor 14 is coaxially connected to the first reduction shaft 154, the first reduction shaft 154 is connected to the sun gear of the planetary gear assembly 151, and the second reduction shaft 155 is connected to the planetary carrier of the planetary gear assembly 151. The first bevel gear 152 is formed or connected to the second reduction shaft 155, and the second bevel gear 153 is formed or connected to the output shaft 12.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0093" num="0088">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">当无刷电机14的电机轴141旋转时，依次通过第一减速轴154、行星轮组件151、第二减速轴155、第一锥齿轮152和第二锥齿轮153，将动力传动至输出轴12处，使得输出轴12能够带动工作附件13转动，工作附件13能够夹持抛光盘(图中未示出)实现对待加工工件的打磨、抛光。</span>When the motor shaft 141 of the brushless motor 14 rotates, the power is transmitted to the output shaft 12 through the first reduction shaft 154, the planetary gear assembly 151, the second reduction shaft 155, the first bevel gear 152 and the second bevel gear 153 in sequence, so that the output shaft 12 can drive the working accessory 13 to rotate, and the working accessory 13 can clamp the polishing disk (not shown in the figure) to grind and polish the workpiece to be processed.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0094" num="0089">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">至于抛光盘，其基本水平设置，抛光盘的直径大于或等于180mm且小于或等于230mm。在一个实施例中，抛光盘的直径为180mm；在一个实施例中，抛光盘的直径为190mm；在一个实施例中，抛光盘的直径为200mm；在一个实施例中，抛光盘的直径为210mm；在一个实施例中，抛光盘的直径为220mm；在一个实施例中，抛光盘的直径为230mm。</span>As for the polishing disc, it is basically arranged horizontally, and the diameter of the polishing disc is greater than or equal to 180 mm and less than or equal to 230 mm. In one embodiment, the diameter of the polishing disc is 180 mm; in one embodiment, the diameter of the polishing disc is 190 mm; in one embodiment, the diameter of the polishing disc is 200 mm; in one embodiment, the diameter of the polishing disc is 210 mm; in one embodiment, the diameter of the polishing disc is 220 mm; in one embodiment, the diameter of the polishing disc is 230 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0095" num="0090">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">控制组件20用于控制无刷电机14并给无刷电机14供电。其中图8至图15所示为控制组件20的第一种结构；图16至图20所示为控制组件20的第二种结构；图21至图26所示为控制组件20的第三种结构。以下对控制组件20的具体结构进行介绍。需要提前说明的是，上述三种结构中的部分部件在控制组件20中可以通用，但是仅在一种结构的附图中进行了展示。</span>The control component 20 is used to control the brushless motor 14 and supply power to the brushless motor 14. Figures 8 to 15 show the first structure of the control component 20; Figures 16 to 20 show the second structure of the control component 20; and Figures 21 to 26 show the third structure of the control component 20. The specific structure of the control component 20 is introduced below. It should be noted in advance that some components in the above three structures can be commonly used in the control component 20, but are only shown in the drawings of one structure.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0096" num="0091">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">具体地，控制组件20包括电路板组件21、电路元件22和控制盒24，电路板组件21和电路元件22均设置在控制盒24内，电路元件22集成在电路板组件21上。为了实现电路板组件21和电路元件22在控制盒24内的固定，将电路元件22安装至电路板组件21上后，将形成的整体放入控制盒24内，并在控制盒24内注入胶体25，以实现电路板组件21和电路元件22在控制盒24内的固定。此外，在控制盒24内注入胶体25还能够起到一定防水防尘的效果，需要说明的是，在控制盒24内注入胶体25后，电路元件22仍然有部分外露在胶外，此部分需要进行防尘处理，所以在电路元件22的外露金属上需要做防护，例如形成密封层，以避免在有水和有粉尘的情况下失效。</span>Specifically, the control assembly 20 includes a circuit board assembly 21, a circuit element 22 and a control box 24. The circuit board assembly 21 and the circuit element 22 are both arranged in the control box 24, and the circuit element 22 is integrated on the circuit board assembly 21. In order to fix the circuit board assembly 21 and the circuit element 22 in the control box 24, after the circuit element 22 is installed on the circuit board assembly 21, the formed whole is placed in the control box 24, and a colloid 25 is injected into the control box 24 to fix the circuit board assembly 21 and the circuit element 22 in the control box 24. In addition, injecting the colloid 25 into the control box 24 can also achieve a certain waterproof and dustproof effect. It should be noted that after the colloid 25 is injected into the control box 24, part of the circuit element 22 is still exposed outside the colloid, and this part needs to be dustproof, so protection needs to be done on the exposed metal of the circuit element 22, such as forming a sealing layer, to avoid failure in the presence of water and dust.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0097" num="0092">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，电路板组件21所在的平面与电机轴141的轴线呈夹角设置。在一个实施例中，电路板组件21所在的平面与电机轴141的轴线基本垂直。</span>In some embodiments, the plane where the circuit board assembly 21 is located is arranged at an angle with the axis of the motor shaft 141. In one embodiment, the plane where the circuit board assembly 21 is located is substantially perpendicular to the axis of the motor shaft 141.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0098" num="0093">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">电路板组件21包括至少一个电路板。在一些实施例中，电路板垂直于电机轴141的轴线方向设置。在一些实施例中，如图8、图18和图23所示，电路板组件21包括两个电路板，两个电路板为相互电连接的第一电路板211和第二电路板212，第一电路板211和第二电路板212基本平行设置，从与第一电路板211相垂直的方向上观察，第一电路板211和第二电路板212至少部分重叠，第一电路板211的面积大于或等于第二电路板212的面积，且如图9所示，控制组件20沿握持部11的延伸方向的最大长度L小于或等于75mm。通过设置两个电路板，使得不同种类的电路元件22可以电连接在不同的电路板上，如此设置减小了控制组件20占用的空间，利于实现该电动工具的小型化。</span>The circuit board assembly 21 includes at least one circuit board. In some embodiments, the circuit board is arranged perpendicular to the axial direction of the motor shaft 141. In some embodiments, as shown in FIG. 8 , FIG. 18 and FIG. 23 , the circuit board assembly 21 includes two circuit boards, the two circuit boards are a first circuit board 211 and a second circuit board 212 electrically connected to each other, the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 are arranged substantially in parallel, and when viewed from a direction perpendicular to the first circuit board 211, the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 at least partially overlap, the area of the first circuit board 211 is greater than or equal to the area of the second circuit board 212, and as shown in FIG. 9 , the maximum length L of the control assembly 20 along the extension direction of the grip 11 is less than or equal to 75 mm. By arranging two circuit boards, different types of circuit elements 22 can be electrically connected to different circuit boards, and such an arrangement reduces the space occupied by the control assembly 20, which is conducive to the miniaturization of the electric tool.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0099" num="0094">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，如图10所示，第一电路板211的最大长度L1小于或等于75mm。在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为72mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为70mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为67mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为65mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为60mm。</span>In some embodiments, as shown in FIG10 , the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is less than or equal to 75 mm. In a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 72 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 70 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 67 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 65 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 60 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0100" num="0095">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，继续参照图10所示，第二电路板212的最大长度L2小于或等于60mm。在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的最大长度L2为58mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的最大长度L2为55mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的最大长度L2为53mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的最大长度L2为51mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的最大长度L2为48mm。</span>In some embodiments, still referring to FIG. 10 , the maximum length L2 of the second circuit board 212 is less than or equal to 60 mm. In a specific embodiment, the maximum length L2 of the second circuit board 212 is 58 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L2 of the second circuit board 212 is 55 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L2 of the second circuit board 212 is 53 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L2 of the second circuit board 212 is 51 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L2 of the second circuit board 212 is 48 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0101" num="0096">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个实施例中，第一电路板211的长度为72mm，且第一电路板211的宽度W为39mm；第二电路板212的长度为60mm，第二电路板212的宽度W为39mm。</span>In one embodiment, the length of the first circuit board 211 is 72 mm, and the width W of the first circuit board 211 is 39 mm; the length of the second circuit board 212 is 60 mm, and the width W of the second circuit board 212 is 39 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0102" num="0097">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，沿握持部11的延伸方向，第一电路板211的最大长度小于或等于75mm。在一些实施例中，沿握持部11的延伸方向，第二电路板212的最大长度L2小于或等于60mm。需要说明的是，沿握持部11的延伸方向，第一电路板211的最大长度与第一电路板211在握持部11内的位姿有关，当第一电路板211平行于握持部11的延伸方向时，沿握持部11的延伸方向第一电路板211的最大长度即为上述L1，当第一电路板211相对于握持部11的延伸方向倾斜设置时，沿握持部11的延伸方向第一电路板211的最大长度等于第一电路板211在握持部11的延伸方向上的投影的长度，该长度小于L1；同理，第二电路板212的最大长度与第二电路板212在握持部11内的位姿有关，当第二电路板212平行于握持部11的延伸方向时，沿握持部11的延伸方向第二电路板212的最大长度即为上述L2，当第二电路板212相对于握持部11的延伸方向倾斜设置时，沿握持部11的延伸方向第二电路板212的最大长度等于第二电路板212在握持部11的延伸方向上的投影的长度，该长度小于L2。</span>In some embodiments, along the extension direction of the grip portion 11, the maximum length of the first circuit board 211 is less than or equal to 75 mm. In some embodiments, along the extension direction of the grip portion 11, the maximum length L2 of the second circuit board 212 is less than or equal to 60 mm. It should be noted that along the extension direction of the grip portion 11, the maximum length of the first circuit board 211 is related to the position of the first circuit board 211 in the grip portion 11. When the first circuit board 211 is parallel to the extension direction of the grip portion 11, the maximum length of the first circuit board 211 along the extension direction of the grip portion 11 is the above-mentioned L1. When the first circuit board 211 is tilted relative to the extension direction of the grip portion 11, the maximum length of the first circuit board 211 along the extension direction of the grip portion 11 is equal to the length of the projection of the first circuit board 211 in the extension direction of the grip portion 11. This length is less than L1; similarly, the maximum length of the second circuit board 212 is related to the position of the second circuit board 212 in the holding portion 11. When the second circuit board 212 is parallel to the extension direction of the holding portion 11, the maximum length of the second circuit board 212 along the extension direction of the holding portion 11 is the above-mentioned L2. When the second circuit board 212 is tilted relative to the extension direction of the holding portion 11, the maximum length of the second circuit board 212 along the extension direction of the holding portion 11 is equal to the length of the projection of the second circuit board 212 in the extension direction of the holding portion 11, which is less than L2.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0103" num="0098">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，第一电路板211的面积小于或等于3000平方毫米。在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2900平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2800平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2700平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2600平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2500平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2400平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2300平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2200平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2100平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的面积为2000平方毫米。</span>In some embodiments, the area of the first circuit board 211 is less than or equal to 3000 square millimeters. In a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2900 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2800 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2700 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2600 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2500 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2400 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2300 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2200 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2100 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the first circuit board 211 is 2000 square millimeters.</span>

<p id="p0104" num="0099">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，第二电路板212的面积小于或等于2500平方毫米。在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的面积为2400平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的面积为2300平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的面积为2200平方毫米；在一个具体的实施例中，第二电路板212的面积为2100平方毫米。</span>In some embodiments, the area of the second circuit board 212 is less than or equal to 2500 square millimeters. In a specific embodiment, the area of the second circuit board 212 is 2400 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the second circuit board 212 is 2300 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the second circuit board 212 is 2200 square millimeters; in a specific embodiment, the area of the second circuit board 212 is 2100 square millimeters.</span>

<p id="p0105" num="0100">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，第一电路板211在抛光盘的抛光平面202的投影面积小于或等于3000平方毫米。</span>In some embodiments, a projection area of the first circuit board 211 on the polishing plane 202 of the polishing plate is less than or equal to 3000 square millimeters.</span>

<p id="p0106" num="0101">
