</p>
<p id="p0107" num="0102">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，在与第一电路板211相垂直的方向上，第一电路板211和第二电路板212重叠部分的面积与第一电路板211的面积的比值为重叠率，其中，重叠率大于或等于50％。在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211和第二电路板212的重叠率为49％；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211和第二电路板212的重叠率为48％；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211和第二电路板212的重叠率为47％；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211和第二电路板212的重叠率为46％；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211和第二电路板212的重叠率为45％。</span>In some embodiments, in a direction perpendicular to the first circuit board 211, the ratio of the area of the overlapping portion of the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 to the area of the first circuit board 211 is the overlap rate, wherein the overlap rate is greater than or equal to 50%. In a specific embodiment, the overlap rate of the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 is 49%; in a specific embodiment, the overlap rate of the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 is 48%; in a specific embodiment, the overlap rate of the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 is 47%; in a specific embodiment, the overlap rate of the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 is 46%; in a specific embodiment, the overlap rate of the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 is 45%.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0108" num="0103">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">进一步地，电路板组件21包括的电路板数量并不局限于两个，根据需求还可以设置为三个、四个或者更多个。在一些实施例中，电路板组件21还包括第三电路板(图中未示出)，从与第一电路板211相垂直的方向上观察，第一电路板211、第二电路板212和第三电路板至少部分重叠，且第一电路板211的面积大于或等于第三电路板的面积。如此设置，能够进一步减少第一电路板211和第二电路板212的尺寸，更利于实现电动工具的小型化。</span>Furthermore, the number of circuit boards included in the circuit board assembly 21 is not limited to two, and can be set to three, four or more according to needs. In some embodiments, the circuit board assembly 21 also includes a third circuit board (not shown in the figure). When viewed from a direction perpendicular to the first circuit board 211, the first circuit board 211, the second circuit board 212 and the third circuit board at least partially overlap, and the area of the first circuit board 211 is greater than or equal to the area of the third circuit board. Such a configuration can further reduce the size of the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212, which is more conducive to miniaturization of the power tool.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0109" num="0104">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">当电路板组件21的电路板的数量为三个时，第一电路板211的最大长度L1可以有效的减少，使得第一电路板211的最大长度L1小于或等于65mm。在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为64mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为63mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为62mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为61mm；在一个具体的实施例中，第一电路板211的最大长度L1为60mm。</span>When the number of circuit boards of the circuit board assembly 21 is three, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 can be effectively reduced, so that the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is less than or equal to 65 mm. In a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 64 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 63 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 62 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 61 mm; in a specific embodiment, the maximum length L1 of the first circuit board 211 is 60 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0110" num="0105">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个实施例中，第一电路板211的长度为61.5mm，第一电路板211的宽度为44mm；第二电路板212的长度为50mm，第二电路板212的宽度为36mm；第三电路板的长度为63mm，第三电路板的宽度为20mm。</span>In one embodiment, the length of the first circuit board 211 is 61.5 mm, and the width of the first circuit board 211 is 44 mm; the length of the second circuit board 212 is 50 mm, and the width of the second circuit board 212 is 36 mm; the length of the third circuit board is 63 mm, and the width of the third circuit board is 20 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0111" num="0106">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">需要说明的是，为了提高控制组件20的结构紧凑性，多个电路板基本均平行设置，控制组件20设置于机壳10内，在一些实施例中，如图8至图20所示，当电动工具处于工作状态时，电路板基本水平设置，并与握持部11的中轴线平行设置；在一些并列的实施例中，当电动工具处于工作状态时，如图21至图26所示，电路板基本竖直设置，并与握持部11的中轴线垂直设置；当然，在其他实施例中，当电动工具处于工作状态时，电路板也可以倾斜设置，并与握持部11的中轴线呈锐角或者钝角设置。</span>It should be noted that in order to improve the structural compactness of the control component 20, multiple circuit boards are basically arranged in parallel, and the control component 20 is arranged in the casing 10. In some embodiments, as shown in Figures 8 to 20, when the power tool is in working condition, the circuit board is basically arranged horizontally and parallel to the central axis of the grip 11; in some parallel embodiments, when the power tool is in working condition, as shown in Figures 21 to 26, the circuit board is basically arranged vertically and perpendicular to the central axis of the grip 11; of course, in other embodiments, when the power tool is in working condition, the circuit board may also be arranged at an inclined angle and be arranged at an acute angle or an obtuse angle to the central axis of the grip 11.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0112" num="0107">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图8所示，电路元件22包括多个电子开关221、整流器222、第二电容223和控制模块，在一些实施例中，多个电子开关221、整流器222和第二电容223均固定在电路板上，需要说明的是，不同种类的电路元件22可以固定在同一块电路板上，也可以固定在不同的电路板上，在一个实施例中，多个电子开关221、整流器222和第二电容223均固定在第一电路板211上，控制模块则设置在第二电路板212上。</span>Continuing with reference to Figure 8, the circuit element 22 includes multiple electronic switches 221, a rectifier 222, a second capacitor 223 and a control module. In some embodiments, the multiple electronic switches 221, the rectifier 222 and the second capacitor 223 are all fixed on the circuit board. It should be noted that different types of circuit elements 22 can be fixed on the same circuit board or on different circuit boards. In one embodiment, the multiple electronic switches 221, the rectifier 222 and the second capacitor 223 are all fixed on the first circuit board 211, and the control module is arranged on the second circuit board 212.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0113" num="0108">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">多个电子开关221用于驱动无刷电机14运行，具体地，多个电子开关221构成三相桥式电路，整流器222构成直流单元，接收电源线17输入的交流电并用于输出直流母线电压，也即用于将通过电源线17输入的交流电转化为脉动直流电输出。控制模块用于控制多个电子开关221的导通状态，从而驱动无刷电机14正常运行，在一些实施例中，控制模块采用控制芯片实现功能。</span>The multiple electronic switches 221 are used to drive the brushless motor 14 to operate. Specifically, the multiple electronic switches 221 form a three-phase bridge circuit, and the rectifier 222 forms a DC unit, which receives the AC power input from the power line 17 and is used to output a DC bus voltage, that is, to convert the AC power input through the power line 17 into a pulsating DC output. The control module is used to control the conduction state of the multiple electronic switches 221, so as to drive the brushless motor 14 to operate normally. In some embodiments, the control module uses a control chip to implement the function.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0114" num="0109">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，电子开关221垂直于电路板。在一些实施例中，电子开关221为IGBT，IGBT代表场效应晶体管；在一些实施例中，电子开关221为MOS；在一些实施例中，电子开关221为FET，FET代表场效应晶体管。</span>In some embodiments, the electronic switch 221 is perpendicular to the circuit board. In some embodiments, the electronic switch 221 is an IGBT, which stands for field effect transistor; in some embodiments, the electronic switch 221 is a MOS; in some embodiments, the electronic switch 221 is a FET, which stands for field effect transistor.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0115" num="0110">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，多个电子开关221在第一电路板211上规律排布，例如可以呈行列排布或者环形排布。在一个实施例中，如图11所示，第一电路板211设置在第二电路板212的上方，电子开关221设置有六个，六个电子开关221分别用221a、221b、221c、221d、221e、221f区分，六个电子开关221呈两行三列排布。整流器222与多个电子开关221在第一电路板211的长度方向上并排设置。第二电容223设置有是三个，其中一个第二电容223设置在电子开关221的一侧，另外两个第二电容223设置在整流器222的两侧，继续参照图11所示，三个第二电容223分别用223a、223b、223c区分。</span>In some embodiments, a plurality of electronic switches 221 are regularly arranged on the first circuit board 211, for example, they can be arranged in rows and columns or in a ring. In one embodiment, as shown in FIG11 , the first circuit board 211 is arranged above the second circuit board 212, and six electronic switches 221 are provided, and the six electronic switches 221 are respectively distinguished by 221a, 221b, 221c, 221d, 221e, and 221f, and the six electronic switches 221 are arranged in two rows and three columns. The rectifier 222 and the plurality of electronic switches 221 are arranged side by side in the length direction of the first circuit board 211. There are three second capacitors 223, one of which is arranged on one side of the electronic switch 221, and the other two second capacitors 223 are arranged on both sides of the rectifier 222. Continuing to refer to FIG11 , the three second capacitors 223 are distinguished by 223a, 223b, and 223c.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0116" num="0111">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些并列的实施例中，如图17至图19所示，第一电路板211设置在第二电路板212的下方，电子开关221、整流器222的数量以及排布不变，第二电容223的数量调整为六个，并设置在第二电路板212上，六个第二电容223呈一行排布。</span>In some parallel embodiments, as shown in Figures 17 to 19, the first circuit board 211 is arranged below the second circuit board 212, the number and arrangement of the electronic switches 221 and the rectifiers 222 remain unchanged, the number of the second capacitors 223 is adjusted to six and arranged on the second circuit board 212, and the six second capacitors 223 are arranged in a row.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0117" num="0112">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些并列的实施例中，如图21至图25所示，电子开关221、整流器222和第二电容223的数量不变，但是排布发生调整，六个电子开关221呈两行三列排布，三个第二电容223设置在两行电子开关221之间，整流器222设置在三个第二电容223的下侧。当然，在其他实施例中，电子开关221、整流器222和第二电容223的排布根据需求以及握持部11内部空间，还可以进行灵活调整。</span>In some parallel embodiments, as shown in FIG. 21 to FIG. 25 , the number of electronic switches 221, rectifiers 222, and second capacitors 223 remains unchanged, but the arrangement is adjusted, and six electronic switches 221 are arranged in two rows and three columns, three second capacitors 223 are arranged between two rows of electronic switches 221, and rectifiers 222 are arranged at the bottom of the three second capacitors 223. Of course, in other embodiments, the arrangement of the electronic switches 221, rectifiers 222, and second capacitors 223 can also be flexibly adjusted according to needs and the internal space of the grip 11.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0118" num="0113">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图8、图18和图22所示，电动工具还包括散热器23，散热器23用于为控制组件20进行散热，散热器23的数量根据需求可以设置为一个或者多个。</span>8 , 18 and 22 , the electric tool further includes a radiator 23 , which is used to dissipate heat for the control component 20 , and the number of the radiator 23 can be set to one or more according to demand.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0119" num="0114">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，继续参照图12至图15所示，在电动工具处于工作状态时，电路板基本均水平设置，电动工具设置有一个散热器23，散热器23位于第一电路板211的下方，且散热器23与多个电子开关221和整流器222的表面接触，电子开关221的第一引脚和整流器222的第二引脚与电路板的背向的一面焊接。散热器23能够实现对电子开关221和整流器222的散热，以避免过热引发故障。当然在其他实施例中，也可以调整第一电路板211和第二电路板212的位置，使得第一电路板211位于第二电路板212的上方，使得散热器23位于第一电路板211的上方。</span>In some embodiments, referring to FIGS. 12 to 15 , when the electric tool is in working state, the circuit boards are basically arranged horizontally, and the electric tool is provided with a heat sink 23, which is located below the first circuit board 211, and the heat sink 23 is in contact with the surfaces of the plurality of electronic switches 221 and the rectifier 222, and the first pin of the electronic switch 221 and the second pin of the rectifier 222 are welded to the back side of the circuit board. The heat sink 23 can achieve heat dissipation for the electronic switch 221 and the rectifier 222 to avoid malfunction caused by overheating. Of course, in other embodiments, the positions of the first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 can also be adjusted so that the first circuit board 211 is located above the second circuit board 212, and the heat sink 23 is located above the first circuit board 211.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0120" num="0115">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图15所示，上述散热器23包括垂直连接的第一散热部232和第二散热部233，第一散热部232基本水平设置，并设置在多个电子开关221和整流器222的上方，第一散热部232上形成多个基本均平行于第一电路板211的风路流道，第二散热部233插入两行电子开关221之间，并与两行电子开关221以及整流器222均接触，如此设置可提高散热效果和散热效率。</span>Continuing with reference to FIG. 15 , the heat sink 23 includes a first heat sink 232 and a second heat sink 233 vertically connected. The first heat sink 232 is basically horizontally arranged and is arranged above a plurality of electronic switches 221 and a rectifier 222. A plurality of air flow channels that are basically parallel to the first circuit board 211 are formed on the first heat sink 232. The second heat sink 233 is inserted between two rows of electronic switches 221 and is in contact with the two rows of electronic switches 221 and the rectifier 222. Such an arrangement can improve the heat dissipation effect and efficiency.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0121" num="0116">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图8和图15所示，为了实现散热器23与电子开关221以及整流器222的固定连接，在电子开关221上设置有第一装配口2211，在整流器222上设置有第二装配口2221，在散热器23上设置有多个第三装配口231，第一装配口2211与第三装配口231一一对应连通，第二装配口2221与第三装配口231一一对应连通，第一连接件穿过第一装配口2211和第三装配口231实现了电子开关221与散热器23的固定，第二连接件穿过第二装配口2221和第三装配口231实现了整流器222与散热器23的固定。第一连接件和第二连接件可以选用螺钉。</span>8 and 15, in order to realize the fixed connection between the heat sink 23 and the electronic switch 221 and the rectifier 222, a first assembly port 2211 is provided on the electronic switch 221, a second assembly port 2221 is provided on the rectifier 222, and a plurality of third assembly ports 231 are provided on the heat sink 23. The first assembly port 2211 is connected to the third assembly port 231 in a one-to-one correspondence, and the second assembly port 2221 is connected to the third assembly port 231 in a one-to-one correspondence. The first connecting member passes through the first assembly port 2211 and the third assembly port 231 to realize the fixation of the electronic switch 221 and the heat sink 23, and the second connecting member passes through the second assembly port 2221 and the third assembly port 231 to realize the fixation of the rectifier 222 and the heat sink 23. The first connecting member and the second connecting member can be screws.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0122" num="0117">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个实施例中，在散热器23的第二散热部233上设置有四个第三装配口231，在每个电子开关221上设置有第一装配口2211，在整流器222上设置有一个第二装配口2221，第一连接件穿过位于第二散热部233一侧的一个电子开关221的第一装配口2211、散热器23上的一个第三装配口231、位于第二散热部233另一侧的另一个电子开关221的第一装配口2211实现散热器23与两个电子开关221的装配，使得仅利用三个第一连接件就能够实现了六个电子开关221与散热器23的固定，而剩余的一个第三装配口231则供第二连接件穿过。</span>In one embodiment, four third assembly openings 231 are provided on the second heat dissipation portion 233 of the heat sink 23, a first assembly opening 2211 is provided on each electronic switch 221, and a second assembly opening 2221 is provided on the rectifier 222. The first connecting member passes through the first assembly opening 2211 of an electronic switch 221 located on one side of the second heat dissipation portion 233, a third assembly opening 231 on the heat sink 23, and the first assembly opening 2211 of another electronic switch 221 located on the other side of the second heat dissipation portion 233 to assemble the heat sink 23 and the two electronic switches 221, so that the six electronic switches 221 and the heat sink 23 can be fixed by only three first connecting members, and the remaining third assembly opening 231 is for the second connecting member to pass through.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0123" num="0118">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些并列的实施例中，如图22至图24所示，在电动工具处于工作状态时，电路板基本均竖直设置，散热器23设置有两个，两个散热器23分别为第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302，第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302分别为每行电子开关221进行散热。</span>In some parallel embodiments, as shown in Figures 22 to 24, when the power tool is in working state, the circuit boards are basically arranged vertically, and two heat sinks 23 are provided. The two heat sinks 23 are respectively a first heat sink 2301 and a second heat sink 2302. The first heat sink 2301 and the second heat sink 2302 respectively dissipate heat for each row of electronic switches 221.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0124" num="0119">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">如图23和图24所示，在一些实施例中，第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302结构相同，第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302均包括第一主体安装板234和散热凸筋235。散热凸筋235包括多个第一散热凸筋2354和多个第二散热凸筋2355。其中，第一主体安装板234为弧形板，第一散热凸筋2354凸设在第一主体安装板234的更靠近电路元件22的一侧，或者说更靠近第二电容223的一侧。相邻两个第一散热凸筋2354之间形成第一风路流道2351，相邻两个第二散热凸筋2355之间形成第二风路流道2352。需要说明的是，在安装第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302时，第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302相对设置，使得两个第一主体安装板234向相反的方向凸设，如此可提高气流流动的顺畅性，从而提高散热效果。</span>As shown in FIG. 23 and FIG. 24, in some embodiments, the first heat sink 2301 and the second heat sink 2302 have the same structure, and both the first heat sink 2301 and the second heat sink 2302 include a first main body mounting plate 234 and a heat dissipation rib 235. The heat dissipation rib 235 includes a plurality of first heat dissipation ribs 2354 and a plurality of second heat dissipation ribs 2355. Among them, the first main body mounting plate 234 is an arc-shaped plate, and the first heat dissipation rib 2354 is convexly arranged on the side of the first main body mounting plate 234 closer to the circuit element 22, or the side closer to the second capacitor 223. A first air path 2351 is formed between two adjacent first heat dissipation ribs 2354, and a second air path 2352 is formed between two adjacent second heat dissipation ribs 2355. It should be noted that when installing the first radiator 2301 and the second radiator 2302, the first radiator 2301 and the second radiator 2302 are arranged relative to each other so that the two first main body mounting plates 234 protrude in opposite directions, which can improve the smoothness of airflow and thus improve the heat dissipation effect.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0125" num="0120">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302的两个散热器23上的风路流道的方向和电路板的板面201倾斜设置。这里的风路流道是指任意两个相邻的散热凸筋235之间形成的供散热风路流通的通道均可成为风路流道。对于一个散热器23而言，可以具有相同的风路流道的方向，也可以具有多个不同的风路流道的方向。本实施例中的第一风路流道2351和第二风路流道2352为两种不同的风路流道的方向。电路板的板面201可以为第一电路板211的板面，也可为第二电路板212的板面。在本实施例中，由于第一电路板211与第二电路板212基本平行，因此图24中以第二电路板212的板面201示意。</span>The directions of the air paths on the two heat sinks 23 of the first heat sink 2301 and the second heat sink 2302 are inclined to the board surface 201 of the circuit board. The air paths here refer to the channels for the heat dissipation air paths formed between any two adjacent heat dissipation ribs 235, which can become air paths. For a heat sink 23, it can have the same direction of the air paths, or it can have multiple different directions of the air paths. In this embodiment, the first air path 2351 and the second air path 2352 are two different directions of the air paths. The board surface 201 of the circuit board can be the board surface of the first circuit board 211, or it can be the board surface of the second circuit board 212. In this embodiment, since the first circuit board 211 is substantially parallel to the second circuit board 212, the board surface 201 of the second circuit board 212 is used as an illustration in FIG24.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0126" num="0121">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">该电动工具通过将散热器23的风路流道和电路板的板面201倾斜设置，不仅利于减少电动工具的径向尺寸，从而便于用户握持操作电动工具，利于实现电动工具的小型化，且对控制组件20具有较佳的散热效果。如图24所示，散热器23的风路流道和电路板的板面201之间所呈夹角用a表示。在图24中，由于第一散热器2301与第二散热器2302结构基本一致，此处的风路流道以第二散热器2302的第一散热凸筋2354形成的风路流道2352进行描述。因此在本方案中，夹角a的一边指代风路流道2352，另一边指代电路板201的板面2112。在一些实施例中，散热器23的风路流道和电路板的板面201之间所呈夹角a大于0°且小于或等于90°。在一个实施例中，散热器23的风路流道和电路板的板面201之间所呈夹角a为90°；在一个实施例中，散热器23的风路流道和电路板的板面201之间所呈夹角a为60°；在一个实施例中，散热器23的风路流道和电路板的板面201之间所呈夹角a为30°。</span>The electric tool is not only conducive to reducing the radial size of the electric tool by tilting the air path of the radiator 23 and the board surface 201 of the circuit board, so as to facilitate the user to hold and operate the electric tool, and to achieve miniaturization of the electric tool, but also has a better heat dissipation effect on the control component 20. As shown in FIG24, the angle between the air path of the radiator 23 and the board surface 201 of the circuit board is represented by a. In FIG24, since the first radiator 2301 and the second radiator 2302 have basically the same structure, the air path here is described by the air path 2352 formed by the first heat dissipation rib 2354 of the second radiator 2302. Therefore, in this scheme, one side of the angle a refers to the air path 2352, and the other side refers to the board surface 2112 of the circuit board 201. In some embodiments, the angle a between the air path of the radiator 23 and the board surface 201 of the circuit board is greater than 0° and less than or equal to 90°. In one embodiment, the angle a between the air flow channel of the heat sink 23 and the board surface 201 of the circuit board is 90°; in one embodiment, the angle a between the air flow channel of the heat sink 23 and the board surface 201 of the circuit board is 60°; in one embodiment, the angle a between the air flow channel of the heat sink 23 and the board surface 201 of the circuit board is 30°.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0127" num="0122">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些并列的实施例中，散热器23的风路流道和电路板的板面201之间所呈夹角a大于30°且小于或等于90°。</span>In some parallel embodiments, the angle a formed between the air passage of the heat sink 23 and the board surface 201 of the circuit board is greater than 30° and less than or equal to 90°.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0128" num="0123">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些并列的实施例中，散热器23的风路流道和电路板的板面201之间所呈夹角a大于50°且小于或等于90°。</span>In some parallel embodiments, the angle a formed between the air passage of the heat sink 23 and the board surface 201 of the circuit board is greater than 50° and less than or equal to 90°.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0129" num="0124">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图23和图24所示，除了第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302外，控制组件20还包括第三散热器2303，第三散热器2303用于为整流器222散热。在一些实施例中，第三散热器2303包括第二主体安装板236和多个第三散热凸筋237，其中，第二主体安装板236为平直板，第二散热凸筋237凸设在第三主体安装板236的外侧，相邻第三散热凸筋237之间形成风路流道。需要说明的是，在安装第二散热器2302和第二散热器2302后，将第三散热器2303安装至第二散热器2302和第二散热器2302的下侧，并使得第三散热凸筋237向下凸设，如此可提高气流流动的顺畅性，从而提高散热效果。</span>Continuing to refer to FIG. 23 and FIG. 24, in addition to the first radiator 2301 and the second radiator 2302, the control assembly 20 further includes a third radiator 2303, which is used to dissipate heat for the rectifier 222. In some embodiments, the third radiator 2303 includes a second main body mounting plate 236 and a plurality of third heat dissipation ribs 237, wherein the second main body mounting plate 236 is a straight plate, the second heat dissipation ribs 237 are convexly arranged on the outer side of the third main body mounting plate 236, and an air path is formed between adjacent third heat dissipation ribs 237. It should be noted that after the second radiator 2302 and the second radiator 2302 are installed, the third radiator 2303 is installed to the lower side of the second radiator 2302 and the second radiator 2302, and the third heat dissipation ribs 237 are convexly arranged downward, so as to improve the smoothness of the air flow, thereby improving the heat dissipation effect.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0130" num="0125">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">需要说明的是，第三散热器2303上形成的风路流道与第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302的风路流道可以平行设置，也可以呈夹角设置。因此，上文关于夹角a的范围同样适用于第三散热器2303。</span>It should be noted that the air passage formed on the third radiator 2303 can be arranged in parallel or at an angle to the air passages of the first radiator 2301 and the second radiator 2302. Therefore, the above range of the angle a also applies to the third radiator 2303.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0131" num="0126">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">如图23和图24所示，为了实现散热器23与电子开关221的固定连接，在电子开关221上设置有第一装配口2211，在第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302上分别设置有多个第三装配口231，第一装配口2211与第三装配口231一一对应连通，第一连接件穿过第一装配口2211和第三装配口231实现了电子开关221与散热器23的固定。</span>As shown in Figures 23 and 24, in order to achieve a fixed connection between the radiator 23 and the electronic switch 221, a first assembly port 2211 is provided on the electronic switch 221, and a plurality of third assembly ports 231 are respectively provided on the first radiator 2301 and the second radiator 2302. The first assembly port 2211 is connected to the third assembly port 231 in a one-to-one correspondence, and the first connecting member passes through the first assembly port 2211 and the third assembly port 231 to achieve the fixation of the electronic switch 221 and the radiator 23.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0132" num="0127">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">为了实现第三散热器2303与整流器222的固定连接，在整流器222上设置有第二装配口2221，在第三散热器2303上设置有第三装配口231，第二装配口2221与第三装配口231一一对应连通，第二连接件穿过第二装配口2221和第三装配口231实现了整流器222与散热器23的固定。</span>In order to achieve a fixed connection between the third radiator 2303 and the rectifier 222, a second assembly port 2221 is provided on the rectifier 222, and a third assembly port 231 is provided on the third radiator 2303. The second assembly port 2221 is connected to the third assembly port 231 in a one-to-one correspondence, and the second connecting member passes through the second assembly port 2221 and the third assembly port 231 to achieve the fixation of the rectifier 222 and the radiator 23.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0133" num="0128">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个实施例中，在第一散热器2301和第二散热器2302上分别设置有三个第三装配口231，在第三散热器2303上设置有一个第三装配口231，在每个电子开关221上设置有第一装配口2211，在整流器222上设置有一个第二装配口2221。</span>In one embodiment, three third assembly openings 231 are respectively provided on the first heat sink 2301 and the second heat sink 2302 , one third assembly opening 231 is provided on the third heat sink 2303 , a first assembly opening 2211 is provided on each electronic switch 221 , and a second assembly opening 2221 is provided on the rectifier 222 .</span>
</p>
<p id="p0134" num="0129">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图23和图24所示，控制组件20还包括第四散热器2304，第四散热器2304集成在控制盒24上，使得控制盒24同时兼具安装功能和散热功能，第一电路板211和第二电路板212均设置在控制盒24内，第四散热器2304包括多个形成在控制盒24周向上的第四散热凸筋，相邻第四散热凸筋之间形成风路流道，需要说明的是，上文关于夹角a的范围同样适用于第四散热器2304。</span>Continuing with reference to Figures 23 and 24, the control component 20 also includes a fourth radiator 2304. The fourth radiator 2304 is integrated on the control box 24, so that the control box 24 has both installation and heat dissipation functions. The first circuit board 211 and the second circuit board 212 are both arranged in the control box 24. The fourth radiator 2304 includes a plurality of fourth heat dissipation ribs formed on the circumference of the control box 24, and air paths are formed between adjacent fourth heat dissipation ribs. It should be noted that the above range of the angle a also applies to the fourth radiator 2304.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0135" num="0130">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">根据控制盒24形状的不同或者握持部11内部空间的形状的不同，电路板的形状可以灵活调整，电路板可以设置为矩形板、圆形板，也可以设置为其他多边形板。当然，也可以如图24所示，电路板为侧壁面由弧形面203和平面202围设形成的非圆形板件204。</span>According to the different shapes of the control box 24 or the different shapes of the internal space of the gripping portion 11, the shape of the circuit board can be flexibly adjusted, and the circuit board can be set as a rectangular plate, a circular plate, or other polygonal plates. Of course, as shown in FIG. 24, the circuit board can also be a non-circular plate 204 formed by the side wall of the arc surface 203 and the plane 202.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0136" num="0131">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个具体的实施例中，电路板通过在垂直于圆形板的径向上切割三次形成的非圆形板件204，其中切割面即为上述平面202，三个平面202分别位于电路板的三个方向，例如可以为上侧、左侧和右侧，或者下侧、左侧和右侧，三个平面202中的两个平面202平行设置，并与剩下的另一个平面202垂直设置。进一步地，该电路板还包括三个弧形面203，每个弧形面203设置在相邻两个平面202之间。</span>In a specific embodiment, the circuit board is cut three times in a radial direction perpendicular to the circular plate to form a non-circular plate 204, wherein the cutting surface is the above-mentioned plane 202, and the three planes 202 are respectively located in three directions of the circuit board, for example, the upper side, the left side and the right side, or the lower side, the left side and the right side, and two of the three planes 202 are arranged in parallel and perpendicular to the remaining plane 202. Further, the circuit board also includes three arcuate surfaces 203, each of which is arranged between two adjacent planes 202.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0137" num="0132">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个具体的实施例中，该非圆形板件204的弧形面203处的直径为51mm；两个相互平行的平面202之间的距离为45mm；剩下的平面202与位于其相对侧的弧形面203之间的距离为48.5mm。在一个具体的实施例中，该非圆形板件204的弧形面203处的直径为51mm；两个相互平行的平面202之间的距离为45mm；剩下的平面202与位于其相对侧的弧形面203之间的距离为46.5mm。</span>In a specific embodiment, the diameter of the curved surface 203 of the non-circular plate 204 is 51 mm; the distance between the two parallel planes 202 is 45 mm; the distance between the remaining plane 202 and the curved surface 203 on the opposite side thereof is 48.5 mm. In a specific embodiment, the diameter of the curved surface 203 of the non-circular plate 204 is 51 mm; the distance between the two parallel planes 202 is 45 mm; the distance between the remaining plane 202 and the curved surface 203 on the opposite side thereof is 46.5 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0138" num="0133">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个具体的实施例中，如图26所示，在电路板上开设有散热孔2111，散热孔2111的设置使得在电路板垂直于握持部11的延伸方向设置时，散热气流能够顺利地通过电路板进行流动，从而保证散热效果。关于散热孔2111的形状和数量根据需求可以灵活设置。</span>In a specific embodiment, as shown in FIG26 , a heat dissipation hole 2111 is provided on the circuit board. The heat dissipation hole 2111 is provided so that when the circuit board is arranged perpendicular to the extension direction of the grip portion 11, the heat dissipation airflow can flow smoothly through the circuit board, thereby ensuring the heat dissipation effect. The shape and number of the heat dissipation holes 2111 can be flexibly set according to requirements.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0139" num="0134">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">如图27所示，抗电磁干扰器件30用于抑制电磁干扰。在一些实施例中，抗电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20分别单独设置，该电动工具抗通过将电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20分别单独设置，使得电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20能够充分利用电动工具内部的空间进行布局，利于实现电动工具的小型化。在一个具体的实施例中，在握持部11的延伸方向上，抗电磁干扰器件30设置在控制组件20的后方。当然，在一些其他的实施例中，抗电磁干扰器件30也可以与控制组件20集成在一起。</span>As shown in FIG. 27 , the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 is used to suppress electromagnetic interference. In some embodiments, the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control component 20 are separately arranged. The electric tool anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control component 20 are separately arranged so that the electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control component 20 can make full use of the space inside the electric tool for layout, which is conducive to the miniaturization of the electric tool. In a specific embodiment, in the extension direction of the grip 11, the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 is arranged behind the control component 20. Of course, in some other embodiments, the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 can also be integrated with the control component 20.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0140" num="0135">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，抗电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20之间的最小距离大于或等于10mm。在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20之间的最小距离为9mm；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20之间的最小距离为8mm；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20之间的最小距离为7mm；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20之间的最小距离为6mm。</span>In some embodiments, the minimum distance between the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control component 20 is greater than or equal to 10 mm. In one embodiment, the minimum distance between the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control component 20 is 9 mm; in one embodiment, the minimum distance between the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control component 20 is 8 mm; in one embodiment, the minimum distance between the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control component 20 is 7 mm; in one embodiment, the minimum distance between the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control component 20 is 6 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0141" num="0136">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图27所示，抗电磁干扰器件30包括抗电磁干扰电路板31、第一电容32、电阻33和电感34，第一电容32、电阻33和电感34均集成在抗电磁干扰电路板31上。</span>Continuing to refer to FIG. 27 , the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 includes an anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 , a first capacitor 32 , a resistor 33 and an inductor 34 . The first capacitor 32 , the resistor 33 and the inductor 34 are all integrated on the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 .</span>
</p>
<p id="p0142" num="0137">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31设置为单板结构。当然，在其他的实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31根据需求还可以设置为多板结构。在一些实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31沿平行于握持部11的延伸方向的方向设置；在一些并列的实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31相较于握持部11的延伸方向倾斜设置。</span>In some embodiments, the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is configured as a single-board structure. Of course, in other embodiments, the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 can also be configured as a multi-board structure according to needs. In some embodiments, the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is arranged in a direction parallel to the extension direction of the grip portion 11; in some parallel embodiments, the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is arranged obliquely compared to the extension direction of the grip portion 11.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0143" num="0138">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的最大长度小于65mm。在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的最大长度为60mm；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的最大长度为58mm；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的最大长度为55mm；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的最大长度为52mm；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的最大长度为40mm。</span>In some embodiments, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is less than 65 mm. In one embodiment, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 60 mm; in one embodiment, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 58 mm; in one embodiment, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 55 mm; in one embodiment, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 52 mm; in one embodiment, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 40 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0144" num="0139">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些并列的实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的最大长度小于55mm。</span>In some parallel embodiments, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is less than 55 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0145" num="0140">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些并列的实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的最大长度小于45mm。</span>In some parallel embodiments, the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is less than 45 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0146" num="0141">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的面积小于或者等于1500平方毫米。在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的面积为1400平方毫米；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的面积为1300平方毫米；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的面积为1200平方毫米；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的面积为1100平方毫米；在一个实施例中，抗电磁干扰电路板31的面积为1000平方毫米。</span>In some embodiments, the area of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is less than or equal to 1500 square millimeters. In one embodiment, the area of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 1400 square millimeters; in one embodiment, the area of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 1300 square millimeters; in one embodiment, the area of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 1200 square millimeters; in one embodiment, the area of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 1100 square millimeters; in one embodiment, the area of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is 1000 square millimeters.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0147" num="0142">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，电阻33为功率NTC电阻，电感34为共模电感。</span>In some embodiments, the resistor 33 is a power NTC resistor, and the inductor 34 is a common mode inductor.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0148" num="0143">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">进一步地，在一些实施例中，抗电磁干扰器件30还包括安装盒，抗电磁干扰电路板31、第一电容32、电阻33和电感34均设置在安装盒36内。在一个实施例中，安装盒36为矩形盒，握持部11的内壁面至少包括安装平面，安装盒36固定在安装平面上。</span>Furthermore, in some embodiments, the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 further includes a mounting box, and the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31, the first capacitor 32, the resistor 33 and the inductor 34 are all arranged in the mounting box 36. In one embodiment, the mounting box 36 is a rectangular box, and the inner wall surface of the gripping portion 11 includes at least a mounting plane, and the mounting box 36 is fixed on the mounting plane.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0149" num="0144">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">需要说明的是，若控制组件20包括控制盒24，抗电磁干扰器件30包括安装盒36，那么抗电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20之间的最小距离是指控制盒24与安装盒36之间的最小距离。若控制组件20不包括控制盒24或抗电磁干扰器件30不包括安装盒36，则以电路板组件21中的电路板或抗电磁干扰电路板31的边界去计算最小距离，而不以电路板上的具体的电路元件去计算最小距离。</span>It should be noted that if the control assembly 20 includes a control box 24 and the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 includes a mounting box 36, then the minimum distance between the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control assembly 20 refers to the minimum distance between the control box 24 and the mounting box 36. If the control assembly 20 does not include the control box 24 or the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 does not include the mounting box 36, the minimum distance is calculated based on the boundary of the circuit board in the circuit board assembly 21 or the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31, rather than the specific circuit elements on the circuit board.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0150" num="0145">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一种实施例中，电路板组件21与抗电磁干扰电路板31之间的最小距离大于或等于5mm。在一种实施例中，电路板组件21与抗电磁干扰电路板31之间的最小距离大于或等于10mm、15mm、20mm、25mm、30mm、35mm、40mm或45mm。电路板组件21与抗电磁干扰电路板31之间的最小距离可以为15mm、20mm、25mm、30mm、35mm、40mm或45mm。</span>In one embodiment, the minimum distance between the circuit board assembly 21 and the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is greater than or equal to 5 mm. In one embodiment, the minimum distance between the circuit board assembly 21 and the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 is greater than or equal to 10 mm, 15 mm, 20 mm, 25 mm, 30 mm, 35 mm, 40 mm or 45 mm. The minimum distance between the circuit board assembly 21 and the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31 may be 15 mm, 20 mm, 25 mm, 30 mm, 35 mm, 40 mm or 45 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0151" num="0146">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，继续参照图27所示，抗电磁干扰器件30还包括交流电插座35，交流电插座35安装至抗电磁干扰电路板31上，抗电磁干扰器件30靠近机壳10的后端设置，电源线17穿过机壳10的后端能够直接与交流电插座35电连接。</span>In some embodiments, continuing with reference to Figure 27, the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 also includes an AC socket 35, which is installed on the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board 31. The anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 is arranged near the rear end of the casing 10, and the power cord 17 passes through the rear end of the casing 10 and can be directly electrically connected to the AC socket 35.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0152" num="0147">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">如图21所示，调速器40用于调节无刷电机14的转速。在一些实施例中，沿握持部11延伸方向上，调速器40和控制组件20至少部分重叠。如此设置使得电动工具内部的结构紧凑，有利于实现电动工具的小型化。</span>As shown in Fig. 21, the speed regulator 40 is used to adjust the speed of the brushless motor 14. In some embodiments, the speed regulator 40 and the control assembly 20 at least partially overlap along the extension direction of the grip portion 11. Such an arrangement makes the internal structure of the power tool compact, which is conducive to miniaturization of the power tool.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0153" num="0148">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图21和图28所示，电动工具还包括供用户操作以控制无刷电机14启停的电机开关18，电机开关18可伸缩的安装至握持部11的下方，通过按压电机开关18能够实现无刷电机14的通电和断电。</span>21 and 28 , the power tool also includes a motor switch 18 for the user to operate to control the start and stop of the brushless motor 14 . The motor switch 18 can be retractably installed under the grip 11 . The brushless motor 14 can be powered on and off by pressing the motor switch 18 .</span>
</p>
<p id="p0154" num="0149">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一些实施例中，电机开关18设置在抗电磁干扰器件30与控制组件20之间。在一些实施例中，调速器40位于电机开关18和无刷电机14之间。</span>In some embodiments, the motor switch 18 is disposed between the anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 and the control assembly 20. In some embodiments, the speed regulator 40 is located between the motor switch 18 and the brushless motor 14.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0155" num="0150">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">如图21所示，该电动工具的整机排布由后至前依次为：电源线17→抗电磁干扰器件30→电机开关18→调速器40→控制组件20→无刷电机14→传动机构15→输出轴12以及工作附件13。</span>As shown in FIG. 21 , the overall arrangement of the power tool from back to front is: power cord 17 → anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 → motor switch 18 → speed regulator 40 → control component 20 → brushless motor 14 → transmission mechanism 15 → output shaft 12 and working accessories 13.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0156" num="0151">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">无刷电机14、控制组件20和抗电磁干扰器件30等在工作过程中会产生大量的热量，为了提高电动工具的散热效果，在机壳10上设置有多个通风口，使得空气能够在电扇的作用下，在电动工具的内外形成气流，以提高散热效果。</span>The brushless motor 14, control component 20 and anti-electromagnetic interference device 30 will generate a large amount of heat during operation. In order to improve the heat dissipation effect of the power tool, a plurality of ventilation holes are arranged on the casing 10 so that air can form airflow inside and outside the power tool under the action of an electric fan to improve the heat dissipation effect.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0157" num="0152">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个实施例中，如图29和图30所示，机壳10上形成位于无刷电机14前侧的第一风口104、位于控制组件20处的第二风口105以及位于握持部11后端的第三风口106，在风扇16作用下形成从第一风口104流入以及从第二风口105和第三风口106流出的散热气流。由于风扇16位于无刷电机14和控制组件20之间，因此从无刷电机14前方进风、从控制组件20后方以及握持部11后端出风，通过风扇16吸风实现对控制组件20的电路板和无刷电机14冷却。</span>In one embodiment, as shown in FIG. 29 and FIG. 30 , the housing 10 is formed with a first air port 104 located at the front side of the brushless motor 14, a second air port 105 located at the control assembly 20, and a third air port 106 located at the rear end of the grip portion 11. A heat dissipation airflow is formed by the fan 16 flowing in from the first air port 104 and flowing out from the second air port 105 and the third air port 106. Since the fan 16 is located between the brushless motor 14 and the control assembly 20, air enters from the front of the brushless motor 14 and exits from the rear of the control assembly 20 and the rear end of the grip portion 11. The fan 16 sucks air to cool the circuit board of the control assembly 20 and the brushless motor 14.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0158" num="0153">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个实施例中，如图29和图31所示，机壳10上形成位于无刷电机14前侧的第一风口104、位于控制组件20处的第二风口105、位于握持部11后端的第三风口106以及与风扇16径向正对的至少一个第四风口107，在风扇16作用下形成从第一风口104、第二风口105和第三风口106流入以及从第四风口107流出的散热气流。由于风扇16位于无刷电机14和控制组件20之间，因此从无刷电机14前方、控制组件20后方以及握持部11后端实现三处进风，并从风扇16的径向实现出风，通过风扇16左右两侧吸风能够实现对控制组件20的电路板和无刷电机14高效冷却。</span>In one embodiment, as shown in FIG. 29 and FIG. 31 , the housing 10 is formed with a first air port 104 located at the front side of the brushless motor 14, a second air port 105 located at the control assembly 20, a third air port 106 located at the rear end of the grip 11, and at least one fourth air port 107 radially opposite to the fan 16. Under the action of the fan 16, a heat dissipation airflow is formed that flows in from the first air port 104, the second air port 105, and the third air port 106 and flows out from the fourth air port 107. Since the fan 16 is located between the brushless motor 14 and the control assembly 20, air is inletted from three locations, namely, the front of the brushless motor 14, the rear of the control assembly 20, and the rear end of the grip 11, and air is discharged from the radial direction of the fan 16. The air suction on the left and right sides of the fan 16 can achieve efficient cooling of the circuit board of the control assembly 20 and the brushless motor 14.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0159" num="0154">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个具体的实施例中，第四风口107设置有多个，多个第四风口107环绕机壳10的周向设置，从而实现多处出风，进一步提高了散热效果。</span>In a specific embodiment, a plurality of fourth air outlets 107 are provided, and the plurality of fourth air outlets 107 are arranged around the circumference of the housing 10 , thereby achieving multiple air outlets and further improving the heat dissipation effect.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0160" num="0155">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">在一个具体的实施例中，第三风口106的进风方向根据需求可以灵活设置，例如第三风口106的进风方向可以平行于握持部11的中轴线，也可以垂直于握持部11的中轴线；当然，第三风口106的进风方向与握持部11的中轴线呈其他角度。此外，第三风口106设置有多个，其中一个第三风口106的进风方向平行于握持部11的中轴线，另一个第三风口106的进风方向垂直于握持部11的中轴线。</span>In a specific embodiment, the air inlet direction of the third air outlet 106 can be flexibly set according to the needs, for example, the air inlet direction of the third air outlet 106 can be parallel to the central axis of the grip portion 11, or can be perpendicular to the central axis of the grip portion 11; of course, the air inlet direction of the third air outlet 106 is at other angles to the central axis of the grip portion 11. In addition, a plurality of third air outlets 106 are provided, wherein the air inlet direction of one third air outlet 106 is parallel to the central axis of the grip portion 11, and the air inlet direction of another third air outlet 106 is perpendicular to the central axis of the grip portion 11.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0161" num="0156">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">为了实现电动工具的小型化，以下对电动工具的尺寸进行限制。继续参照图9所示，机壳10的尾部到输出轴12中心线的距离为第一长度L3，第一长度L3小于或等于390mm。需要说明的是，第一长度L3是指不包含偏心的输出轴12距离，输出轴12可以安装具有偏心结构的偏心块，然后再安装抛光盘，这里的第一长度L3不包括偏心距。</span>In order to achieve miniaturization of the power tool, the size of the power tool is limited as follows. Continuing to refer to FIG. 9 , the distance from the tail of the housing 10 to the center line of the output shaft 12 is the first length L3, and the first length L3 is less than or equal to 390 mm. It should be noted that the first length L3 refers to the distance of the output shaft 12 excluding the eccentricity. The output shaft 12 can be installed with an eccentric block with an eccentric structure, and then a polishing disk is installed. The first length L3 here does not include the eccentricity.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0162" num="0157">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图9所示，机壳10的尾部到定子142前端的距离为第二长度L4，第一长度L4小于或等于280mm。在一个实施例中，第二长度L4为279mm；在一个实施例中，第二长度L4为275mm；在一个实施例中，第二长度L4为270mm。</span>9, the distance from the rear of the housing 10 to the front end of the stator 142 is the second length L4, and the first length L4 is less than or equal to 280 mm. In one embodiment, the second length L4 is 279 mm; in one embodiment, the second length L4 is 275 mm; in one embodiment, the second length L4 is 270 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0163" num="0158">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图9所示，机壳10的尾部到机壳10的头部的距离为电动工具的整体长度L5，电动工具的整体长度L5小于或等于450mm。在一个实施例中，电动工具的整体长度L5为446mm；在一个实施例中，电动工具的整体长度L5为440mm；在一个实施例中，电动工具的整体长度L5为420mm；在一个实施例中，电动工具的整体长度L5为400mm。</span>Continuing to refer to FIG9 , the distance from the rear of the housing 10 to the head of the housing 10 is the overall length L5 of the power tool, and the overall length L5 of the power tool is less than or equal to 450 mm. In one embodiment, the overall length L5 of the power tool is 446 mm; in one embodiment, the overall length L5 of the power tool is 440 mm; in one embodiment, the overall length L5 of the power tool is 420 mm; in one embodiment, the overall length L5 of the power tool is 400 mm.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0164" num="0159">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">继续参照图3所示，电动工具在电机开关18处的最大高度为第一高度D3，第一高度D3小于或等于63mm。而电动工具的机壳10在电机开关18处的高度为第二高度D4，第一高度D4小于或等于52mm。需要说明的是，可以理解为，第一高度D3为第二高度D4与电机开关18凸出机壳10的高度的总和。</span>Continuing to refer to FIG. 3 , the maximum height of the electric tool at the motor switch 18 is a first height D3, which is less than or equal to 63 mm. The height of the housing 10 of the electric tool at the motor switch 18 is a second height D4, which is less than or equal to 52 mm. It should be noted that it can be understood that the first height D3 is the sum of the second height D4 and the height of the motor switch 18 protruding from the housing 10.</span>
</p>
<p id="p0165" num="0160">
<span class="notranslate"> <span class="google-src-text">以上显示和描述了本申请的基本原理、主要特征和优点。本行业的技术人员应该了解，上述实施例不以任何形式限制本申请，凡采用等同替换或等效变换的方式所获得的技术方案，均落在本申请的保护范围内。</span>The above shows and describes the basic principles, main features and advantages of the present application. Those skilled in the art should understand that the above embodiments do not limit the present application in any form, and any technical solution obtained by equivalent replacement or equivalent transformation falls within the protection scope of the present application.</span>
</p>

<div class="claim-text">10. The power tool of claim 1, wherein the maximum length of the anti-electromagnetic interference circuit board is less than 45mm.</div>
